name:R‚Äça‚Äçj‚Äçd‚Äçe‚Äçe‚Äçp‚Äç ‚ÄçM‚Äça‚Äça‚Äçn
info:Executive River View King Room
info:Stayed in July 2021
info:Solo travelers
info:2 Reviews
rating:4.5
posted:Posted August 1, 2021
msg:The hotel stay here was perfectly adequate the room was clean, the staff perfectly polite and attentive. But a few points of feedback for the hotel. In certain areas the hotel lacked a 5* level of quality service. Mostly during breakfast. The first morning I arrived to breakfast around 10am and the hotel staff let me enter and have breakfast. After arriving it was clear that. The service was coming to an end so I am not sure why this wasn't explained with things being taken away. I was confused to why they let me enter when I couldn't eat anything. 

The following day I arrived earlier for service and after scanning my room key I was left to myself. When I have stayed in other hotels of 5* quality normally you are taken to a seat and offered a hot drink as a minimum. Normally I wouldn't complain about this but given the hotel and the star rating these bits of service feel quite basic and missing. Despite the above the breakfast offer is large and things I ate all tastes good and were to a.high quality a good mix of western and eastern options 

The hotel did have a luxury feeling but it felt empty from a design point and had a dated or aged feeling of luxury. My room was very comfortable and clean etc. But it felt empty especially in the bathroom due to how it was designed and laid out. For example I couldn't find any light switches by the door to my room just do not disturb switch. The bed room lights were next to the bed. When coming back late and it's dark you have make your way into the room to turn the lights on. An odd design choice. 

As mentioned above these are not things I would normally complain about but when paying to stay at a hotel under the brand you have certain expectations and attention to detail is key. 

Despite being hard on the hotel in my stay I would stay here again and encourage others to do the same. It is a nice hotel just requires greater attention to detail.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Deluxe River-view Twin Room
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:4 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted April 21, 2024
msg:This is the most satisfactory hotel I have stayed in recently. The location is perfect. It takes only two minutes to walk from Qiushui Square Station on Line 1. It is extremely convenient to travel. There are also many shopping malls nearby, so it is very convenient to go shopping and eat.
The room is very comfortable, the quilt is not too thick, and my mother can rarely fall asleep without waking up in the middle of the night due to the heat. The bed is also very soft and hard. And it is a river view room, which is not a discount at all. The whole floor-to-ceiling window faces the Ganjiang River and Tengwang Pavilion. The Qiushui Square Music Fountain is downstairs. You can squat in front of the window at night to enjoy the whole performance. It is perfect.
The buffet breakfast is great, with a wide variety. The freshly made fried buns are delicious, with a thin and crispy bottom and delicious fillings. It is worth a net celebrity store outside. Zhou Zhenzhen's mixed noodles and clay pot soup are both worth recommending, as well as freshly made pancakes with fried dough sticks and bacon. In addition, Western-style omelets, baked puddings, pork floss bread, etc. are all good, and the fruits are also sweet. The milk, yogurt, and freshly squeezed juice are all online, and Xiao Wei's service is very good. After eating this breakfast at 8 o'clock in the morning, I went to visit the museum for four hours without any problems.
Check-in and check-out are very convenient, and the elevator is very fast. I personally think the price-performance ratio is very high. Next time I come to Nanchang, I will definitely stay at this hotel!

msg:All five-star reviews. Some people say that this hotel is old and outdated. I must refute it: Although the hotel is a little old, it is well maintained. There is no problem living there. It is clean and tidy. It is not bad because it is old. Tengwang Pavilion across the river is even older. Don't you want to go there?
The overlooking scenery is magnificent. The breakfast is very rich and of high quality. It is a five-star standard. It is worth the room fee.
The next is the suggestion: the hotel's business philosophy also needs to keep pace with the times. There are many old and large hotels that have not changed their habits: a deposit is required. As the best hotel in Nanchang, the tourists who come here must not only have accommodation needs, but also spiritual needs. The deposit is paid before registration, which makes the guests feel untrusted. It is not a roadside shop. The quality of the guests is low. Beware of each other. This grace should be maintained.
There are all kinds of charged snacks in the room. It is really unnecessary. It may be too much to say that it is free, but it is unnecessary to put them in the room. The pattern is small, and the times have changed. Customers' demand in this regard is on the verge of extinction. They can't sell a few a day. It's a real feeling, for reference only.

msg:Usually when I go to a certain city for the first time, I will definitely choose an internationally renowned chain brand, which can make people feel more at ease. This was my first time going to Nanchang and I chose Nanchang Xiang without hesitation.
The location is more convenient for transportation, just outside Qiushui Square on the subway. It is convenient to take a taxi to both high-speed rail stations. Next to it is the Ganjiang River. The river view room faces the Ganjiang River. You can watch the light show of Qiushui Square in the room at night without having to go downstairs to brave the cold wind.
The lobby is very grand and spacious.
The room is quite satisfactory, and as many reviews said, it would be more convenient if there was a tissue box in the room.
What follows are some encounters.
1. The inner frame of the door is broken. The inner door frame can be pulled down directly by hanging the anti-theft chain. After calling, I sent a technician from the engineering depar**ent to come and repair it. All they did was knock the door frame tight. . Then there is no more.
If I were the one to deal with this, I would at least give you a phone call to check back after the repair is completed. If the guest is a single female and living together, I will ask if it is necessary to change rooms, because after all, the door frame is just knocked in, and it will still be pushed open if pushed hard from the outside.
2. The inner wall of the bathtub fell off, and pieces of it floated away after the water was drained.
3. I won‚Äôt talk about other things. It‚Äôs not easy for everyone to work part-time.
Logically speaking, a hotel that has been in business for 15 years should not do so.
I got a call the night before check-in to ask about arrival time and special requests, and I also called on the day of check-out to ask about the check-in experience. I also reported on the phone the problem with the door frame and the question about how to deal with it, but then nothing happened again hahaha

msg:A family of three stayed at Shangri-La Hotel, Nanchang for the summer vacation, and I must say, the experience was impressive.

First of all, the hotel facilities are amazing. The room is spacious and bright, with luxurious and elegant decoration, and the bed is extremely comfortable, so you can enjoy a high-quality sleep every night. The bathroom is well-equipped, spacious and bright, and the water pressure of the shower is just right, making washing up a pleasure. In addition, the public areas of the hotel are equally impressive, whether it is the lobby or the restaurant, they all appear very high-end. There are also resident singers at night, which is perfect for having a drink~~~~

We booked two deluxe river view rooms with extremely wide views. Looking out the windows of the room, we have a panoramic view of the magnificent Ganjiang River. Tengwang Pavilion stands on the bank of the river, and the scenery on both sides is charming.

In the morning, as the sun rises, the Tengwang Pavilion on the Ganjiang River is dyed with a touch of gold, making it look like a dream. At night, the lights of Tengwang Pavilion are bright, like a shining pearl, which makes people feel respectful. One of them is themed with an Egyptian cute god. My baby likes it very much~~~~~

Hygiene wise, the hotel's cleanliness standards are very high. The room was thoroughly cleaned every day and the sheets and towels were fresh, which was very reassuring. I was very pleased with how spotlessly clean every corner of the hotel was.

What impressed me most was the hotel service. The staff was very professional and friendly, always available and quickly addressed all my needs and questions. Whether it was front desk reception or restaurant service, they all performed at a very high level and made me feel at home.

The receptionist attitude of the check-in Particularly good, very smooth check into the room. The room is really big with a small sofa and a computer desk. The oversized bathroom is just great. My favorite is the two big windows looking at the river and the night view of Nanchang at night (the fountain in Qiushui Square can be seen directly in the room) . The location of Shangri-La Hotel is also unique. I have never stayed in a five-star hotel so close to the subway. It takes two minutes to the subway station (Qiushui Square Station). Some scenic spots are directly accessible, which makes my trip to Nanchang more convenient. The breakfast is also great, with both Chinese and Western classic cuisines, as well as local specialty snacks in Nanchang (I really like crock soup), which is very satisfying. Finally, Miss Luo Tingting, who checked out, asked about our housing experience, and the check-out procedure was smooth and quick. In short, Shangri-La Hotel will undoubtedly make my trip to Nanchang the icing on the cake, and I will choose Shangri-La Hotel next time!
